### Type Definitions

- **Brand** — Homepage, pricing, product pages, templates gallery, careers, partners
- **Transactional** — Sign-in, sign-up, checkout, forms, legal pages
- **Content** — /tips/ and /blog/ editorial pages (see content breakdown below)
- **Education** — university.flodesk.com courses and resources
- **Docs** — developers.flodesk.com, grain.flodesk.com
- **Support** — help.flodesk.com
- **User-generated** — view.flodesk.com previews, usercontent.flodesk.com PDFs
- **Other** — Campaign shortlinks, uncategorized
